0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;"> &#8211; HealthEquity, Inc. (NASDAQ&#58; HQY) (&#34;HealthEquity&#34; or the &#34;Company&#34;), the nation's largest health savings account (&#34;HSA&#34;) non-bank custodian, today announced financial results for its second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2020, compared to its prior quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019, which did not include the acquisition of WageWorks.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8220;The HealthEquity team delivered strong results this quarter despite the pandemic. Adjusted EBITDA of $60 million, a sequential increase in adjusted EBITDA margin to 34%, and robust sales speak to the margin and growth opportunities of our business,&#8221; said Jon Kessler, President and CEO of HealthEquity. &#8220;Team Purple delivered for our members, clients and partners, growing HSA Assets sequentially by over $700 million, a second quarter record, and maintaining the high level of service HealthEquity is known for even as 97% of team members worked from home.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Second quarter financial results</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Revenue for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2020 of $176.0&#160;million grew 103% compared to $86.6&#160;million for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019. Revenue this quarter included&#58; service revenue of $103.8&#160;million, custodial revenue of $46.9&#160;million, and interchange revenue of $25.3&#160;million. </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity reported a net loss of $0.1&#160;million, or less than one half of one cent per diluted share, and non-GAAP net income of $30.1&#160;million, or $0.42 per diluted share, for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2020. The Company reported net income of $19.4&#160;million, or $0.30 per diluted share, and non-GAAP net income of $28.8&#160;million, or $0.44 per diluted share, for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Adjusted EBITDA was $60.0&#160;million for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2020, an increase of 48% compared to $40.6&#160;million for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019. Adjusted EBITDA was 34% of revenue compared to 47% for the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Account and asset metrics</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HSAs as of July&#160;31, 2020 were approximately 5.4&#160;million, an increase of 29% year over year, including 284,000 HSAs with investments, an increase of 52% year over year. Total Accounts as of July&#160;31, 2020 were 12.5&#160;million, including 7.1&#160;million consumer-directed benefit (&#34;CDB&#34;) accounts.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Total HSA Assets as of July&#160;31, 2020 were $12.2&#160;billion, an increase of 43% year over year. Total HSA Assets included $9.0&#160;billion of HSA cash and $3.2&#160;billion of HSA investments. Client-held funds, which are deposits held on behalf of our Clients to facilitate administration of our CDBs, and from which we generate custodial revenue, were $0.8&#160;billion as of July&#160;31, 2020.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">New HSA openings and HSA asset balances</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity reported sales of 108,000 new HSAs in the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2020, compared to 126,000 in the second quarter ended July&#160;31, 2019. HSA members grew their cash balances by approximately $246.0&#160;million during the quarter, while total member balances increased by approximately $707.0&#160;million due primarily to decreased spending per HSA and appreciation of invested balances.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font><br></font></div><div style="position:relative;width:100%;height:54pt;"><div style="position:absolute;bottom:0;width:100%;"><div style="text-align:center;-sec-extract:summary;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:54pt;width:100%;"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">WageWorks integration and increased synergy target</font></div><div><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity completed its acquisition of WageWorks on August 30, 2019. The Company accelerated its integration efforts and achieved its previously stated goal of $50 million in run rate synergies by the end of this second quarter, more than a year ahead of schedule. We also successfully migrated five legacy platforms and approximately $1 billion in HSA assets to our legacy HealthEquity HSA platform. In addition, we completed the return of all service calls to the United States.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">In light of this progress, the Company raised its net synergy target to $80 million, to be achieved over the next 18 months.  Said Ted Bloomberg, Chief Operating Officer of HealthEquity, &#8220;Consolidating to a single platform for the delivery of our total solution will enable our members, clients and partners to better connect health and wealth, while increasing the efficiency and focus of our team.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Business outlook</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">For the fiscal year ending January 31, 2021, management expects revenues of $720 million to $730 million. Its outlook is for net loss between $13 million and $5 million, resulting in net loss per diluted share of $0.17 to $0.08. Its outlook for non-GAAP net income, calculated using the method described below, is between $111 million and $119 million, resulting in non-GAAP net income per diluted share of $1.48 to $1.58 (based on an estimated 75 million weighted-average shares outstanding). Management expects Adjusted EBITDA of $226 million to $236 million.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">See &#8220;Non-GAAP financial information&#8221; below for definitions of our Adjusted EBITDA and non-GAAP net income. A reconciliation of the non-GAAP financial measures used throughout this release to the most comparable GAAP financial measures is included with the financial tables at the end of this release.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Conference call</font></div><div><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;">HealthEquity management will host a conference call at 4&#58;30 pm (Eastern Time) on Tuesday, September 8, 2020 to discuss the second quarter 2021 financial results. The conference call will be accessible by dialing 844-791-6252, or 661-378-9636 for international callers, and referencing conference ID 5170518. A live audio webcast of the call will also be available on the investor relations section of our website at http&#58;&#47;&#47;ir.healthequity.com.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Non-GAAP financial information </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">To supplement our financial information presented on a GAAP basis, we disclose non-GAAP financial measures, including Adjusted EBITDA, non-GAAP net income, and non-GAAP net income per diluted share. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Adjusted EBITDA is adjusted earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization, amortization of acquired intangible assets, stock-based compensation expense, merger integration and acquisition-related costs, gains and losses on marketable equity securities, and other certain non-operating items. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Non-GAAP net income is calculated by adding back to net income before provision for income taxes the following items&#58; amortization of acquired intangible assets, stock-based compensation expense, merger integration and acquisition-related costs, and gains and losses on marketable equity securities.</font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Non-GAAP net income per diluted share is calculated by dividing non-GAAP net income by diluted weighted-average shares outstanding.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, We believe that these&#160;non-GAAP&#160;financial measures provide useful information to management and investors regarding certain financial and business trends relating to the Company's financial condition and results of operations. The Company cautions investors that non-GAAP financial information, by its nature, departs from GAAP&#59; accordingly, its use can make it difficult to compare current results with results from other reporting periods and with the results of other companies.
